// === FILE: hiveant/core/kernel/runtime.nc ===
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  HiveANT — Swarm OS Kernel: Agent Runtime
//
//  The kernel manages agent lifecycle, scheduling, resource quotas,
//  and inter-agent communication. Agents behave like lightweight
//  OS processes with spawn/kill/suspend/resume semantics.
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to kernel_init:
    purpose: "Initialize the HiveANT kernel and all subsystems"
    shell("mkdir -p incidents knowledge docs memory/pheromone memory/twins memory/tasks agents_state")

    set kernel_state to {
        "version": "1.0.0",
        "name": "HiveANT",
        "started_at": time_iso(time_now()),
        "agents": {},
        "agent_count": 0,
        "max_agents": 10000,
        "clusters": {},
        "cluster_count": 0,
        "tick": 0,
        "status": "running"
    }
    write_file("agents_state/kernel.json", json_encode(kernel_state))
    log "KERNEL: HiveANT initialized"
    respond with kernel_state

to kernel_status:
    purpose: "Return current kernel state and agent census"
    if file_exists("agents_state/kernel.json"):
        try:
            set state to json_decode(read_file("agents_state/kernel.json"))
            set state.agent_count to shell("ls agents_state/agent-*.json 2>/dev/null | wc -l || echo 0")
            set state.uptime_seconds to time_now() - state.started_at
            respond with state
        otherwise:
            respond with {"error": "Corrupt kernel state file"}
    otherwise:
        respond with {"error": "Kernel not initialized. Call POST /kernel/init first."}

to spawn_agent with agent_type, agent_id:
    purpose: "Spawn a new agent process in the swarm"
    if file_exists("agents_state/kernel.json") is not equal true:
        respond with {"error": "Kernel not initialized", "_status": 500}

    try:
        set k_state to json_decode(read_file("agents_state/kernel.json"))
    otherwise:
        respond with {"error": "Corrupt kernel state", "_status": 500}

    if agent_id is not equal "":
        set aid to agent_id
    otherwise:
        set aid to agent_type + "-" + str(floor(random() * 9000 + 1000))

    set agent to {
        "id": aid,
        "type": agent_type,
        "status": "running",
        "spawned_at": time_iso(time_now()),
        "last_heartbeat": time_iso(time_now()),
        "tasks_completed": 0,
        "tasks_failed": 0,
        "memory_usage_kb": 0,
        "cpu_ticks": 0,
        "cluster_id": "default"
    }

    write_file("agents_state/agent-" + aid + ".json", json_encode(agent))
    set k_state.agent_count to k_state.agent_count + 1
    write_file("agents_state/kernel.json", json_encode(k_state))

    log "KERNEL: Spawned agent " + aid + " (type=" + agent_type + ")"
    respond with agent

to kill_agent with agent_id:
    purpose: "Terminate an agent process"
    set path to "agents_state/agent-" + agent_id + ".json"
    if file_exists(path):
        try:
            set agent to json_decode(read_file(path))
            set agent.status to "terminated"
            set agent.terminated_at to time_iso(time_now())
            write_file(path, json_encode(agent))

            set agent_count to shell("ls agents_state/agent-*.json 2>/dev/null | wc -l || echo 0")
            try:
                set k_state to json_decode(read_file("agents_state/kernel.json"))
                set k_state.agent_count to agent_count
                write_file("agents_state/kernel.json", json_encode(k_state))
            otherwise:
                log "WARN: Could not update kernel state"

            log "KERNEL: Killed agent " + agent_id
            respond with {"agent_id": agent_id, "status": "terminated"}
        otherwise:
            respond with {"error": "Corrupt agent file", "_status": 500}
    otherwise:
        respond with {"error": "Agent not found", "_status": 404}

to suspend_agent with agent_id:
    purpose: "Suspend an agent (pause execution)"
    set path to "agents_state/agent-" + agent_id + ".json"
    if file_exists(path):
        try:
            set agent to json_decode(read_file(path))
            set agent.status to "suspended"
            set agent.suspended_at to time_iso(time_now())
            write_file(path, json_encode(agent))
            log "KERNEL: Suspended agent " + agent_id
            respond with {"agent_id": agent_id, "status": "suspended"}
        otherwise:
            respond with {"error": "Corrupt agent file", "_status": 500}
    otherwise:
        respond with {"error": "Agent not found", "_status": 404}

to resume_agent with agent_id:
    purpose: "Resume a suspended agent"
    set path to "agents_state/agent-" + agent_id + ".json"
    if file_exists(path):
        try:
            set agent to json_decode(read_file(path))
            set agent.status to "running"
            set agent.resumed_at to time_iso(time_now())
            write_file(path, json_encode(agent))
            log "KERNEL: Resumed agent " + agent_id
            respond with {"agent_id": agent_id, "status": "running"}
        otherwise:
            respond with {"error": "Corrupt agent file", "_status": 500}
    otherwise:
        respond with {"error": "Agent not found", "_status": 404}

to list_agents with status_filter:
    purpose: "List all agents, optionally filtered by status"
    set result to shell("ls agents_state/agent-*.json 2>/dev/null || echo NONE")
    if result is equal "NONE":
        respond with {"agents": [], "count": 0}

    set agents to []
    set files to split(result, "\n")
    repeat for each f in files:
        if file_exists(f):
            try:
                set data to json_decode(read_file(f))
                if status_filter:
                    if data.status is equal status_filter:
                        set agents to agents + [data]
                otherwise:
                    set agents to agents + [data]
            otherwise:
                log "WARN: Corrupt agent file " + f
                continue

    respond with {"agents": agents, "count": len(agents)}

to agent_heartbeat with agent_id, metrics:
    purpose: "Record agent heartbeat with resource metrics"
    set path to "agents_state/agent-" + agent_id + ".json"
    if file_exists(path):
        try:
            set agent to json_decode(read_file(path))
            set agent.last_heartbeat to time_iso(time_now())
            if metrics:
                set agent.memory_usage_kb to metrics.memory_kb
                set agent.cpu_ticks to metrics.cpu_ticks
            write_file(path, json_encode(agent))
            respond with {"agent_id": agent_id, "heartbeat": "ok"}
        otherwise:
            respond with {"error": "Corrupt agent file", "_status": 500}
    otherwise:
        respond with {"error": "Agent not found", "_status": 404}

// === FILE: hiveant/core/message_bus/message_bus.nc ===
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  HiveANT — Distributed Message Bus
//
//  Enables inter-agent communication. Agents publish/subscribe
//  to topics. Supports broadcast, direct, and cluster messaging.
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to bus_publish with topic, message, sender_id:
    purpose: "Publish a message to a topic"
    shell("mkdir -p agents_state/bus")
    set msg to {"topic": topic, "message": message, "sender": sender_id, "timestamp": time_now(), "id": "MSG-" + str(floor(random() * 90000 + 10000))}
    set topic_file to "agents_state/bus/topic-" + topic + ".json"

    if file_exists(topic_file):
        set existing to read_file(topic_file)
        set msgs to json_decode(existing)
    otherwise:
        set msgs to {"messages": [], "subscriber_count": 0}

    set msgs.messages to msgs.messages + [msg]
    write_file(topic_file, json_encode(msgs))
    log "BUS: Published to " + topic + " by " + str(sender_id)
    respond with {"published": true, "topic": topic, "msg_id": msg.id}

to bus_subscribe with topic, agent_id:
    purpose: "Subscribe an agent to a topic"
    shell("mkdir -p agents_state/bus")
    set sub_file to "agents_state/bus/subs-" + topic + ".json"
    if file_exists(sub_file):
        set subs to json_decode(read_file(sub_file))
    otherwise:
        set subs to {"topic": topic, "subscribers": []}

    set subs.subscribers to subs.subscribers + [agent_id]
    write_file(sub_file, json_encode(subs))
    respond with {"subscribed": true, "topic": topic, "agent_id": agent_id}

to bus_read with topic, since:
    purpose: "Read messages from a topic"
    set topic_file to "agents_state/bus/topic-" + topic + ".json"
    if file_exists(topic_file):
        set data to json_decode(read_file(topic_file))
        respond with data
    otherwise:
        respond with {"messages": [], "topic": topic}

to bus_direct with target_agent, message, sender_id:
    purpose: "Send a direct message to a specific agent"
    shell("mkdir -p agents_state/bus/direct")
    set msg to {"message": message, "sender": sender_id, "timestamp": time_now()}
    set inbox to "agents_state/bus/direct/" + target_agent + ".json"
    if file_exists(inbox):
        set existing to json_decode(read_file(inbox))
    otherwise:
        set existing to {"inbox": []}
    set existing.inbox to existing.inbox + [msg]
    write_file(inbox, json_encode(existing))
    respond with {"sent": true, "to": target_agent}

to bus_topics:
    purpose: "List all active topics"
    set result to shell("ls agents_state/bus/topic-*.json 2>/dev/null | while read f; do basename \"$f\" .json | sed 's/topic-//'; done || echo NONE")
    if result is equal "NONE":
        respond with {"topics": [], "count": 0}
    set topics to split(trim(result), "\n")
    respond with {"topics": topics, "count": len(topics)}

// === FILE: hiveant/core/scheduler/scheduler.nc ===
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  HiveANT — Swarm Scheduler
//
//  Distributes tasks to agents using priority queues.
//  Tracks task assignments, deadlines, retries, and load balancing.
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to scheduler_init:
    purpose: "Initialize the scheduler subsystem"
    shell("mkdir -p agents_state/queue")
    set sched to {
        "initialized_at": time_now(),
        "tasks_queued": 0,
        "tasks_dispatched": 0,
        "tasks_completed": 0,
        "tasks_failed": 0,
        "max_retries": 3,
        "queue": []
    }
    write_file("agents_state/scheduler.json", json_encode(sched))
    log "SCHEDULER: Initialized"
    respond with sched

to enqueue_task with task_id, task_type, priority, payload, assigned_agent:
    purpose: "Add a task to the scheduler queue"
    if file_exists("agents_state/scheduler.json") is not equal true:
        respond with {"error": "Scheduler not initialized"}

    set sched to json_decode(read_file("agents_state/scheduler.json"))

    if task_id:
        set tid to task_id
    otherwise:
        set tid to task_type + "-" + str(floor(random() * 90000 + 10000))

    if priority:
        set p to priority
    otherwise:
        set p to 5

    set task to {
        "task_id": tid,
        "type": task_type,
        "priority": p,
        "status": "queued",
        "payload": payload,
        "assigned_agent": assigned_agent,
        "created_at": time_now(),
        "retries": 0,
        "result": ""
    }

    write_file("agents_state/queue/" + tid + ".json", json_encode(task))
    set sched.tasks_queued to sched.tasks_queued + 1
    write_file("agents_state/scheduler.json", json_encode(sched))

    log "SCHEDULER: Queued task " + tid + " (type=" + task_type + ", priority=" + str(p) + ")"
    respond with task

to dispatch_tasks:
    purpose: "Dispatch queued tasks to available agents"
    set queued to shell("ls agents_state/queue/*.json 2>/dev/null || echo NONE")
    if queued is equal "NONE":
        respond with {"dispatched": 0, "message": "No tasks in queue"}

    set dispatched to 0
    set files to split(trim(queued), "\n")
    repeat for each f in files:
        if file_exists(trim(f)) is not equal true:
            skip
        set task to json_decode(read_file(trim(f)))
        if task.status is equal "queued":
            if task.assigned_agent:
                set agent_path to "agents_state/agent-" + task.assigned_agent + ".json"
                if file_exists(agent_path):
                    set agent to json_decode(read_file(agent_path))
                    if agent.status is equal "running":
                        set task.status to "dispatched"
                        set task.dispatched_at to time_now()
                        write_file(f, json_encode(task))
                        set dispatched to dispatched + 1
            otherwise:
                set task.status to "dispatched"
                set task.dispatched_at to time_now()
                write_file(f, json_encode(task))
                set dispatched to dispatched + 1

    set sched to json_decode(read_file("agents_state/scheduler.json"))
    set sched.tasks_dispatched to sched.tasks_dispatched + dispatched
    write_file("agents_state/scheduler.json", json_encode(sched))

    log "SCHEDULER: Dispatched " + str(dispatched) + " tasks"
    respond with {"dispatched": dispatched}

to complete_task with task_id, result, success:
    purpose: "Mark a task as completed or failed"
    set path to "agents_state/queue/" + task_id + ".json"
    if file_exists(path):
        set task to json_decode(read_file(path))
        set sched to json_decode(read_file("agents_state/scheduler.json"))
        if success is equal "yes":
            set task.status to "completed"
            set task.result to result
            set task.completed_at to time_now()
            set sched.tasks_completed to sched.tasks_completed + 1
        otherwise:
            set task.retries to task.retries + 1
            if task.retries is above sched.max_retries:
                set task.status to "failed"
                set task.result to result
                set sched.tasks_failed to sched.tasks_failed + 1
            otherwise:
                set task.status to "queued"
                log "SCHEDULER: Retrying task " + task_id + " (attempt " + str(task.retries) + ")"
        write_file(path, json_encode(task))
        write_file("agents_state/scheduler.json", json_encode(sched))
        respond with task
    otherwise:
        respond with {"error": "Task not found", "_status": 404}

to scheduler_status:
    purpose: "Get scheduler statistics"
    if file_exists("agents_state/scheduler.json"):
        set sched to json_decode(read_file("agents_state/scheduler.json"))
        respond with sched
    otherwise:
        respond with {"error": "Scheduler not initialized"}

// === FILE: hiveant/core/stability/stability.nc ===
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  HiveANT — Swarm Stability Mechanisms
//
//  Prevents uncontrolled swarm behavior with:
//    - Max agents per task limits
//    - Spawn depth limits
//    - Task timeout policies
//    - Duplicate task detection
//    - Agent conflict resolution
//    - Runaway swarm detection & termination
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to stability_init with config:
    purpose: "Initialize swarm stability parameters"
    shell("mkdir -p agents_state")

    if config:
        set params to config
    otherwise:
        set params to {"max_agents_total": 1000, "max_agents_per_task": 20, "max_spawn_depth": 4, "task_timeout_seconds": 300, "duplicate_detection": true, "conflict_resolution": "priority", "runaway_threshold_per_minute": 50}

    write_file("agents_state/stability_config.json", json_encode(params))
    log "STABILITY: Initialized with max_agents=" + str(params.max_agents_total) + " max_per_task=" + str(params.max_agents_per_task)
    respond with params

to stability_check_spawn with agent_type, task_id, depth:
    purpose: "Check if spawning a new agent is safe"
    set config_path to "agents_state/stability_config.json"
    if file_exists(config_path):
        set cfg to json_decode(read_file(config_path))
    otherwise:
        set cfg to {"max_agents_total": 1000, "max_agents_per_task": 20, "max_spawn_depth": 4}

    set total_agents to shell("ls agents_state/agent-*.json 2>/dev/null | wc -l || echo 0")
    set total to trim(total_agents)

    if total is above cfg.max_agents_total:
        respond with {"allowed": false, "reason": "Total agent limit reached (" + str(cfg.max_agents_total) + ")", "total_agents": total}

    if depth:
        if depth is above cfg.max_spawn_depth:
            respond with {"allowed": false, "reason": "Max spawn depth exceeded (" + str(cfg.max_spawn_depth) + ")", "depth": depth}

    respond with {"allowed": true, "total_agents": total, "limits": cfg}

to stability_detect_runaway:
    purpose: "Detect and terminate runaway swarm behavior"
    set config_path to "agents_state/stability_config.json"
    if file_exists(config_path):
        set cfg to json_decode(read_file(config_path))
    otherwise:
        set cfg to {"runaway_threshold_per_minute": 50}

    set recent_spawns to shell("ls -lt agents_state/agent-*.json 2>/dev/null | head -60 | wc -l || echo 0")
    set spawn_count to trim(recent_spawns)

    if spawn_count is above cfg.runaway_threshold_per_minute:
        log "STABILITY WARNING: Potential runaway swarm detected (" + str(spawn_count) + " agents)"
        respond with {"runaway_detected": true, "agent_count": spawn_count, "threshold": cfg.runaway_threshold_per_minute, "action": "Consider killing excess agents"}
    otherwise:
        respond with {"runaway_detected": false, "agent_count": spawn_count, "threshold": cfg.runaway_threshold_per_minute}

to stability_status:
    purpose: "Get swarm stability status"
    set config_path to "agents_state/stability_config.json"
    if file_exists(config_path):
        set cfg to json_decode(read_file(config_path))
        set total to shell("ls agents_state/agent-*.json 2>/dev/null | wc -l || echo 0")
        respond with {"config": cfg, "current_agents": trim(total), "healthy": true}
    otherwise:
        respond with {"status": "not_initialized"}

// === FILE: hiveant/core/task_graph/task_graph.nc ===
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  HiveANT — Task Graph Engine
//
//  All work is structured as directed acyclic graphs (DAGs).
//  Each investigation creates a goal node that decomposes into
//  subtasks. Agents claim tasks from the graph rather than
//  generating arbitrary work.
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

to create_task_graph with goal, description, subtasks:
    purpose: "Create a new task graph rooted at a goal"
    shell("mkdir -p memory/tasks")

    set graph_id to "TG-" + str(floor(random() * 90000 + 10000))

    set nodes to []
    set goal_node to {
        "id": graph_id + "-ROOT",
        "type": "goal",
        "description": goal,
        "status": "pending",
        "children": [],
        "created_at": time_now()
    }

    if subtasks:
        set idx to 0
        repeat for each st in subtasks:
            set child_id to graph_id + "-T" + str(idx)
            set child to {
                "id": child_id,
                "type": "task",
                "description": st.description,
                "agent_type": st.agent_type,
                "status": "pending",
                "parent": goal_node.id,
                "dependencies": st.dependencies,
                "priority": st.priority,
                "created_at": time_now()
            }
            set nodes to nodes + [child]
            set goal_node.children to goal_node.children + [child_id]
            set idx to idx + 1

    set graph to {
        "graph_id": graph_id,
        "goal": goal,
        "description": description,
        "status": "active",
        "root": goal_node,
        "nodes": nodes,
        "created_at": time_now(),
        "completed_at": ""
    }

    write_file("memory/tasks/" + graph_id + ".json", json_encode(graph))
    log "TASK_GRAPH: Created " + graph_id + " with " + str(len(nodes)) + " subtasks"
    respond with graph

to get_task_graph with graph_id:
    purpose: "Retrieve a task graph by ID"
    set path to "memory/tasks/" + graph_id + ".json"
    if file_exists(path):
        respond with json_decode(read_file(path))
    otherwise:
        respond with {"error": "Task graph not found", "_status": 404}

to claim_task with graph_id, task_id, agent_id:
    purpose: "Agent claims a task from the graph"
    set path to "memory/tasks/" + graph_id + ".json"
    if file_exists(path):
        set graph to json_decode(read_file(path))
        set found to false
        set idx to 0
        repeat for each node in graph.nodes:
            if node.id is equal task_id:
                if node.status is equal "pending":
                    set node.status to "in_progress"
                    set node.claimed_by to agent_id
                    set node.claimed_at to time_now()
                    set graph.nodes[idx] to node
                    set found to true
                otherwise:
                    respond with {"error": "Task already claimed", "status": node.status}
            set idx to idx + 1

        if found:
            write_file(path, json_encode(graph))
            log "TASK_GRAPH: Agent " + agent_id + " claimed " + task_id
            respond with {"task_id": task_id, "agent_id": agent_id, "status": "in_progress"}
        otherwise:
            respond with {"error": "Task not found in graph"}
    otherwise:
        respond with {"error": "Graph not found", "_status": 404}

to complete_graph_task with graph_id, task_id, result:
    purpose: "Mark a task in the graph as completed"
    set path to "memory/tasks/" + graph_id + ".json"
    if file_exists(path):
        set graph to json_decode(read_file(path))
        set idx to 0
        repeat for each node in graph.nodes:
            if node.id is equal task_id:
                set node.status to "completed"
                set node.result to result
                set node.completed_at to time_now()
                set graph.nodes[idx] to node
            set idx to idx + 1

        set all_done to true
        repeat for each node in graph.nodes:
            if node.status is not equal "completed":
                set all_done to false

        if all_done:
            set graph.status to "completed"
            set graph.completed_at to time_now()
            log "TASK_GRAPH: All tasks complete for " + graph_id

        write_file(path, json_encode(graph))
        respond with {"task_id": task_id, "status": "completed", "graph_complete": all_done}
    otherwise:
        respond with {"error": "Graph not found", "_status": 404}

to generate_investigation_graph with service_name, description:
    purpose: "Auto-generate a standard investigation task graph"
    set subtasks to [
        {"description": "Analyze system logs for errors and anomalies", "agent_type": "investigation", "dependencies": [], "priority": 1},
        {"description": "Collect and analyze metrics (latency, error rate, CPU, memory)", "agent_type": "investigation", "dependencies": [], "priority": 1},
        {"description": "Inspect service dependency graph for cascading failures", "agent_type": "investigation", "dependencies": [], "priority": 2},
        {"description": "Review recent deployments and configuration changes", "agent_type": "investigation", "dependencies": [], "priority": 2},
        {"description": "Run ant colony root cause analysis on causal paths", "agent_type": "root_cause", "dependencies": ["T0", "T1", "T2", "T3"], "priority": 3},
        {"description": "Generate remediation strategies via bee colony optimization", "agent_type": "fix_generation", "dependencies": ["T4"], "priority": 4},
        {"description": "Validate proposed fix in sandbox environment", "agent_type": "validation", "dependencies": ["T5"], "priority": 5},
        {"description": "Store incident knowledge and update pheromone scores", "agent_type": "learning", "dependencies": ["T6"], "priority": 6}
    ]

    set goal to "Investigate anomaly in " + service_name + ": " + description
    set graph_id to "TG-" + str(floor(random() * 90000 + 10000))

    set nodes to []
    set goal_node to {
        "id": graph_id + "-ROOT",
        "type": "goal",
        "description": goal,
        "status": "pending",
        "children": [],
        "created_at": time_now()
    }

    set idx to 0
    repeat for each st in subtasks:
        set child_id to graph_id + "-T" + str(idx)
        set child to {
            "id": child_id,
            "type": "task",
            "description": st.description,
            "agent_type": st.agent_type,
            "status": "pending",
            "parent": goal_node.id,
            "dependencies": st.dependencies,
            "priority": st.priority,
            "created_at": time_now()
        }
        set nodes to nodes + [child]
        set goal_node.children to goal_node.children + [child_id]
        set idx to idx + 1

    set graph to {
        "graph_id": graph_id,
        "goal": goal,
        "description": description,
        "service": service_name,
        "status": "active",
        "root": goal_node,
        "nodes": nodes,
        "created_at": time_now(),
        "completed_at": ""
    }

    write_file("memory/tasks/" + graph_id + ".json", json_encode(graph))
    log "TASK_GRAPH: Generated investigation graph " + graph_id + " for " + service_name
    respond with graph

to list_task_graphs:
    purpose: "List all task graphs"
    set result to shell("ls memory/tasks/TG-*.json 2>/dev/null || echo NONE")
    if result is equal "NONE":
        respond with {"graphs": [], "count": 0}
    set graphs to []
    set files to split(trim(result), "\n")
    repeat for each f in files:
        if file_exists(trim(f)) is not equal true:
            skip
        try:
            set data to json_decode(read_file(trim(f)))
            set graphs to graphs + [{"graph_id": data.graph_id, "goal": data.goal, "status": data.status, "node_count": len(data.nodes), "created_at": data.created_at}]
        otherwise:
            log "WARN: Could not parse task graph file: " + f
    respond with {"graphs": graphs, "count": len(graphs)}

// === FILE: hiveant/docs/API_REFERENCE.md ===
# HiveANT — API Reference

**62 endpoints** | Base URL: `https://hiveant.devheallabs.in` (or `http://localhost:7700` local)
Content-Type: `application/json`
Authentication: JWT Bearer token (for write endpoints)

---

## Core

### `GET /health`
Basic health check.
```json
// Response
{"status": "healthy", "service": "hiveant", "version": "1.0.0"}
```

### `POST /kernel/init`
Initialize all subsystems (kernel, scheduler, pheromone DB, digital twin).
```json
// Response
{
  "kernel": {"version": "1.0.0", "name": "HiveANT", "status": "running", ...},
  "scheduler": "initialized",
  "pheromone_db": "initialized",
  "digital_twin": "initialized",
  "message": "HiveANT is ready."
}
```

### `GET /kernel/status`
Full system status including all subsystems.
```json
// Response
{
  "system": "HiveANT",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "kernel": {"agent_count": "3", "uptime_seconds": 1200, ...},
  "scheduler": {"tasks_queued": 0, "tasks_completed": 5, ...},
  "pheromone_graph": {"edge_count": 12, "reinforcements": 4},
  "digital_twin": {"services": 3, "dependencies": 5},
  "incidents": "7"
}
```

### `GET /config`
Show connected data sources (secrets masked).

---

## Agents

### `POST /agents/spawn`
```json
// Request
{"agent_type": "detection", "agent_id": "det-001", "config": {}}
// agent_type: detection|investigation|root_cause|fix_generation|validation|learning|prediction|scout|worker|evaluator

// Response
{"id": "det-001", "type": "detection", "status": "running", "spawned_at": 1773460000.0, ...}
```

### `POST /agents/kill`
```json
// Request
{"agent_id": "det-001"}

// Response
{"agent_id": "det-001", "status": "terminated"}
```

### `GET /agents`
List all agents. Optional query: `?status_filter=running`

---

## Investigation Pipeline

### `POST /investigate`
Full swarm investigation: collects telemetry, runs ACO root cause analysis, runs ABC fix optimization, saves incident report.
```json
// Request
{"service_name": "checkout-api", "description": "HTTP 500 errors since 15:42 UTC"}

// Response
{
  "incident_id": "INC-4821",
  "service": "checkout-api",
  "root_cause": "Database credential mismatch after deploy v2.4.1",
  "confidence": 92,
  "category": "configuration",
  "causal_chain": [...],
  "evidence_chain": [...],
  "remediation": {"recommended_fix": {...}},
  ...
}
```

### `POST /self-heal`
Diagnose and optionally auto-fix.
```json
// Request
{
  "service_name": "checkout-api",
  "description": "HTTP 500 errors",
  "auto_execute": "yes",
  "secret": "your-heal-secret"
}

// Response
{
  "incident_id": "HEAL-3291",
  "root_cause": "...",
  "auto_executed": "yes",
  "execution_results": [{"command": "...", "result": "..."}],
  "verification": "..."
}
```

### `POST /watchdog`
Check all MONITOR_URLS for health.

---

## Swarm Algorithms

### `POST /swarm/ant/explore`
Run ACO causal path exploration.
```json
// Request
{"signals": "[{\"name\":\"high_error_rate\",\"evidence\":\"94%\"}]", "system_context": "checkout-api after deploy"}

// Response
{
  "best_path": {"path": ["deploy_v2.4.1", "credential_mismatch", "connection_failure"], "confidence": 0.89},
  "root_cause_candidates": [...],
  "pheromone_updates": [...]
}
```

### `POST /swarm/bee/optimize`
Run ABC remediation optimization.
```json
// Request
{"root_cause": "DB credential mismatch", "system_context": "checkout-api, PostgreSQL"}

// Response
{
  "recommended_fix": {
    "solution_id": "FIX-001",
    "category": "config",
    "description": "Update database credentials to match new secret manager values",
    "commands": [...],
    "confidence_percent": 88
  },
  "alternative_fixes": [...]
}
```

---

## Intelligence

### `POST /causal/analyze`
Bayesian causal reasoning.
```json
// Request
{"events": "[...]", "system_context": "..."}
```

### `POST /observe`
Observability intelligence (anomaly detection, trends).
```json
// Request
{"service_name": "checkout-api", "time_window": "1h"}
```

// === FILE: hiveant/docs/CONFIGURATION.md ===
# HiveANT — Configuration Guide

**Domain**: [https://hiveant.devheallabs.in](https://hiveant.devheallabs.in)

All configuration is done through environment variables. Copy `config/.env.example` to `config/.env` and customize.

> **Important**: Use the NC binary from `nc-main/nc/build/nc` (not `notation-as-code`).

---

## Required Variables

| Variable | Default | Description |
|----------|---------|-------------|
| `NC_ALLOW_EXEC` | — | **Must be `1`**. Allows shell commands. Without this, health checks and kubectl fail silently. |
| `NC_ALLOW_FILE_WRITE` | — | **Must be `1`**. Allows file writes. Without this, ALL state is silently lost (incidents, agents, knowledge). |
| `NC_AI_URL` | — | AI model API endpoint. Examples: `http://localhost:11434/v1/chat/completions` (Ollama), `https://api.openai.com/v1/chat/completions` (OpenAI) |
| `NC_AI_MODEL` | — | Model name. Examples: `llama3`, `gpt-4`, `claude-3-opus` |
| `NC_AI_KEY` | — | API key for the AI provider. Use `local` for Ollama. |

---

## Server Configuration

| Variable | Default | Description |
|----------|---------|-------------|
| `HIVEANT_PORT` | `7700` | HTTP server port (note: currently hardcoded in server.nc; env var is for documentation) |

---

## Integration Variables (Optional)

| Variable | Default | Description |
|----------|---------|-------------|
| `PROMETHEUS_URL` | — | Prometheus base URL. Example: `http://prometheus:9090` |
| `ELASTICSEARCH_URL` | — | Elasticsearch base URL. Example: `http://elasticsearch:9200` |
| `GITHUB_TOKEN` | — | GitHub personal access token for deploy history |
| `GITHUB_REPO` | — | GitHub repo in `owner/repo` format |
| `JAEGER_URL` | — | Jaeger query API URL for distributed tracing |
| `SLACK_WEBHOOK` | — | Slack incoming webhook URL for incident notifications |
| `MONITOR_URLS` | — | Comma-separated health check URLs. Example: `http://api:8080/health,http://web:3000/health` |

---

## Security Variables

| Variable | Default | Description |
|----------|---------|-------------|
| `HEAL_SECRET` | — | Shared secret required for self-heal and rollback operations. Set to a strong random value. |
| `SANDBOX_ENABLED` | `true` | Whether to require sandbox validation before production changes |
| `MAX_ACTIONS_PER_MINUTE` | `60` | Per-agent rate limit for destructive actions |
| `REQUIRE_APPROVAL_FOR` | `high-risk` | Risk level that requires human approval (`low`, `medium`, `high-risk`) |

---

## Swarm Algorithm Parameters

### Ant Colony Optimization (ACO)

| Variable | Default | Description |
|----------|---------|-------------|
| `ANT_COLONY_SIZE` | `50` | Number of simulated ants per exploration |
| `ANT_MAX_ITERATIONS` | `100` | Maximum ACO iterations |
| `ANT_ALPHA` | `1.0` | Pheromone influence weight |
| `ANT_BETA` | `2.0` | Heuristic influence weight |
| `ANT_EVAPORATION` | `0.1` | Pheromone evaporation rate per cycle |

### Artificial Bee Colony (ABC)

| Variable | Default | Description |
|----------|---------|-------------|
| `BEE_SCOUT_COUNT` | `10` | Number of scout bees |
| `BEE_WORKER_COUNT` | `30` | Number of worker bees |
| `BEE_EVALUATOR_COUNT` | `10` | Number of evaluator bees |
| `BEE_MAX_CYCLES` | `50` | Maximum ABC optimization cycles |
| `BEE_ABANDONMENT_LIMIT` | `5` | Cycles before abandoning a food source |

---

## Pheromone Graph

| Variable | Default | Description |
|----------|---------|-------------|
| `PHEROMONE_DECAY_RATE` | `0.05` | Score reduction per evaporation cycle |
| `PHEROMONE_REINFORCE_AMOUNT` | `1.0` | Score increase on successful discovery |
| `PHEROMONE_MIN_THRESHOLD` | `0.01` | Minimum score before edge is removed |

---

## Swarm Stability

| Variable | Default | Description |
|----------|---------|-------------|
| `HIVEANT_MAX_AGENTS` | `10000` | Maximum total agents across all clusters |
| `HIVEANT_CLUSTERS` | `100` | Number of swarm clusters |
| `HIVEANT_AGENTS_PER_CLUSTER` | `100` | Agent capacity per cluster |

---

## Reinforcement Learning

| Variable | Default | Description |
|----------|---------|-------------|
| `RL_ALPHA` | `0.1` | Learning rate for Q-value updates |
| `RL_EPSILON` | `0.2` | Exploration rate (decays over time) |
| `SELF_HEAL_CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD` | `70` | Minimum confidence % to auto-execute fixes |

---

## Kubernetes (when deployed in-cluster)

| Variable | Default | Description |
|----------|---------|-------------|
| `K8S_NAMESPACE` | `default` | Default Kubernetes namespace |
| `K8S_IN_CLUSTER` | `false` | Whether running inside K8s (for ServiceAccount auth) |

---

## Data Files

HiveANT stores all state as JSON files in these directories (relative to working directory):

| Directory | Contents | Backed Up? |
|-----------|----------|------------|
| `incidents/` | Incident reports (INC-*, HEAL-*, ALERT-*) | Should be backed up |
| `knowledge/` | Learned patterns, RL policy, runbooks | Should be backed up |
| `memory/pheromone/edges/` | Pheromone graph edges | Should be backed up |
| `memory/twins/` | Digital twin model | Should be backed up |
| `memory/tasks/` | Task graphs | Can be regenerated |
| `agents_state/` | Agent records, kernel state | Regenerated on restart |
| `agents_state/audit/` | Audit trail | Should be backed up |
| `simulation/results/` | Simulation outputs | Optional |

### Backup

```bash
# Simple backup
tar czf hiveant-backup-$(date +%Y%m%d).tar.gz incidents/ knowledge/ memory/ agents_state/audit/

# Restore
tar xzf hiveant-backup-YYYYMMDD.tar.gz
```

// === FILE: hiveant/docs/DEPENDENCIES.md ===
# HiveANT — Dependencies

Everything you need to install to make HiveANT work.

---

## Quick Status on Your Machine

| Dependency | Status | Action |
|-----------|--------|--------|
| macOS (ARM64) | Installed | None |
| Xcode CLI Tools | Installed | None |
| C compiler (cc/gcc) | Installed | None |
| make | Installed | None |
| curl | Installed | None |
| Homebrew | Installed | None |
| kubectl | Installed | None |
| NC Engine | Built at `notation as code/nc/build/nc` | Need to add to PATH |
| Ollama | **NOT INSTALLED** | Required for local AI |

---

## Tier 1 — REQUIRED (HiveANT won't start without these)

### 1. NC Engine (the runtime)

NC is already built on your machine. You just need it in your PATH:

```bash
# Option A: Symlink (recommended)
sudo ln -sf "/Users/NuckalaSai.Narender4/Documents/notation as code/nc/build/nc" /usr/local/bin/nc

# Option B: Copy
sudo cp "/Users/NuckalaSai.Narender4/Documents/notation as code/nc/build/nc" /usr/local/bin/nc

# Verify
nc version
```

**Build dependencies** (if you ever need to rebuild NC):
- C11 compiler (cc/gcc/clang) — you have this
- make — you have this
- libcurl — comes with macOS
- libm — comes with macOS
- pthreads — comes with macOS

### 2. AI Model (the brain)

HiveANT needs an AI model to reason about incidents. Pick ONE:

#### Option A: Ollama (LOCAL — recommended for production, no API costs)

```bash
# Install Ollama
brew install ollama

# Start Ollama service
ollama serve &

# Pull a model (pick one)
ollama pull llama3          # 4.7GB — good balance
ollama pull llama3:70b      # 40GB — best quality, needs 64GB RAM
ollama pull mistral         # 4.1GB — fast, good for testing
ollama pull codellama       # 3.8GB — better for code analysis
ollama pull phi3            # 2.3GB — smallest, fastest

# Verify
curl http://localhost:11434/api/tags
```

Then set in your `.env`:
```bash
NC_AI_URL=http://localhost:11434/v1/chat/completions
NC_AI_MODEL=llama3
NC_AI_KEY=local
```

#### Option B: OpenAI API (REMOTE — fastest setup, costs money)

```bash
# No install needed — just set your API key
NC_AI_URL=https://api.openai.com/v1/chat/completions
NC_AI_MODEL=gpt-4o
NC_AI_KEY=sk-your-key-here
```

Cost: ~$0.01-0.10 per investigation (3 AI calls per investigation)

#### Option C: Anthropic Claude (REMOTE — via OpenAI-compatible proxy)

```bash
# Use a proxy like LiteLLM
pip install litellm
litellm --model claude-3-5-sonnet-20241022 --port 4000 &

NC_AI_URL=http://localhost:4000/v1/chat/completions
NC_AI_MODEL=claude-3-5-sonnet-20241022
NC_AI_KEY=sk-ant-your-key
```

#### Option D: Any OpenAI-compatible API

HiveANT works with any API that accepts the OpenAI chat completions format:
- vLLM
- text-generation-inference
- LocalAI
- LM Studio
- Together AI
- Groq
- Fireworks AI

### 3. Environment Variables

```bash
# Create config
cp config/.env.example config/.env

# MINIMUM required in config/.env:
NC_ALLOW_EXEC=1           # Let NC run shell commands
NC_ALLOW_FILE_WRITE=1     # Let NC write files (CRITICAL)
NC_AI_URL=<your-ai-url>   # AI endpoint
NC_AI_MODEL=<model-name>  # Model to use
NC_AI_KEY=<your-key>      # API key (or "local" for Ollama)
```

---

## Tier 2 — OPTIONAL (features work without these, just show "not configured")

### Prometheus (metrics monitoring)

```bash
# Install
brew install prometheus

# Or Docker
docker run -d -p 9090:9090 prom/prometheus

# Set in .env
PROMETHEUS_URL=http://localhost:9090
```

### Elasticsearch (log search)

```bash
# Docker (easiest)
docker run -d -p 9200:9200 -e "discovery.type=single-node" \
  -e "xpack.security.enabled=false" \
  docker.elastic.co/elasticsearch/elasticsearch:8.12.0

# Set in .env
ELASTICSEARCH_URL=http://localhost:9200
```

### GitHub (deployment history)

```bash
# Generate a personal access token at https://github.com/settings/tokens
# Scopes needed: repo (read)

# Set in .env
GITHUB_TOKEN=ghp_your_token_here
GITHUB_REPO=your-org/your-repo
```

### Slack (incident notifications)

```bash
# Create incoming webhook at https://api.slack.com/messaging/webhooks

# Set in .env
SLACK_WEBHOOK=https://hooks.slack.com/services/T.../B.../xxx
```

### Jaeger (distributed tracing)

```bash
# Docker
docker run -d -p 16686:16686 -p 6831:6831/udp jaegertracing/all-in-one

# Set in .env
JAEGER_URL=http://localhost:16686
```

### Kubernetes (container orchestration)

```bash
# Already installed on your machine (kubectl found)
# For local K8s cluster:
brew install minikube
minikube start

# Or use Docker Desktop's built-in K8s
```

---

## Tier 3 — DEVELOPMENT ONLY

### Docker (for containerized deployment)

```bash
brew install --cask docker
# Or: https://docs.docker.com/desktop/install/mac-install/
```

### Docker Compose (for full stack)

```bash
# Included with Docker Desktop
# Or standalone:
brew install docker-compose
```

---

## Dependency Matrix

| Dependency | Required? | What breaks without it |
|-----------|-----------|----------------------|
| NC Engine | **YES** | Nothing runs |
| AI Model (any) | **YES** | No investigations, no reasoning, no predictions |
| `NC_ALLOW_EXEC=1` | **YES** | shell() calls silently fail |
| `NC_ALLOW_FILE_WRITE=1` | **YES** | ALL data silently lost |
| curl | **YES** | Health checks, watchdog fail |
| bash | **YES** | shell() commands fail |
| Prometheus | No | Metrics show "not configured" |
| Elasticsearch | No | Logs show "not configured" |
| GitHub token | No | Deploy history shows "not configured" |
| Slack webhook | No | No incident notifications |
| Jaeger | No | No trace analysis |
| kubectl | No | No K8s management |
| Docker | No | Can't run containerized |

---

## One-Command Setup

Run this to install everything and start HiveANT:

```bash
./scripts/setup.sh
```

// === FILE: hiveant/docs/DEVELOPER_GUIDE.md ===
# HiveANT Developer Guide

This guide covers everything needed to understand, extend, and contribute to HiveANT.

---

## Table of Contents

1. [Project Structure](#project-structure)
2. [How Agents Work](#how-agents-work)
3. [Swarm Algorithms](#swarm-algorithms)
4. [Cognitive Memory System](#cognitive-memory-system)
5. [Digital Twin](#digital-twin)
6. [Adding a New Agent](#adding-a-new-agent)
7. [Adding a New Integration](#adding-a-new-integration)
8. [API Reference](#api-reference)
9. [Testing Guide](#testing-guide)

---

## Project Structure

```
hiveant/
|
|-- server.nc                 Main HTTP server. All 63 routes defined here.
|                             Loads all modules, handles auth, dispatches to agents.
|
|-- start.sh / start.bat     Main entry point scripts for all platforms.
|
|-- config/
|   |-- .env.example          Template with all configurable environment variables.
|   +-- .env                  Active configuration (not committed).
|
|-- core/                     Kernel layer -- the foundation.
|   |-- kernel/runtime.nc     Agent lifecycle: spawn, run, kill, state persistence.
|   |                         Manages agents_state/ directory on disk.
|   |-- scheduler/scheduler.nc  Task queue and dispatch. Assigns tasks to agents
|   |                           based on type and availability.
|   |-- task_graph/task_graph.nc  DAG-based task decomposition. Breaks complex
|   |                             investigations into subtasks with dependencies.
|   |-- message_bus/message_bus.nc  Pub/sub inter-agent communication.
|   |                               Topics stored in agents_state/bus/.
|   +-- stability/stability.nc  Swarm safety: max agent limits, spawn depth,
|                               duplicate detection, runaway termination.
|
|-- swarm/                    Swarm intelligence algorithms.
|   |-- ant_colony/ant_colony.nc   ACO implementation. Agents explore causal
|   |                              paths. Pheromone reinforcement on success.
|   |-- bee_colony/bee_colony.nc   ABC implementation. Scout/Worker/Evaluator
|   |                              phases for fix optimization.
|   +-- clustering/clustering.nc   Hierarchical clustering for 10,000+ agents.
|                                  Divides agents into regional clusters with
|                                  a global coordinator.
|
|-- agents/                   All 12 agent types.
|   |-- detection/            Monitors health, detects anomalies. Entry point
|   |                         for the investigation pipeline.
|   |-- investigation/        Collects logs (Elasticsearch), metrics (Prometheus),
|   |                         traces (Jaeger), deploy history (GitHub).
|   |-- root_cause/           ACO-based causal path analysis. Produces a
|   |                         root cause with confidence score.
|   |-- fix_generation/       ABC-based remediation. Generates fix commands
|   |                         with alternatives and risk assessment.
|   |-- validation/           Sandbox tests fixes before production. Dry-run
|   |                         execution with safety analysis.
|   |-- learning/             Updates cognitive memory after incident resolution.
|   |                         Feeds RL Q-table with outcome data.
|   |-- prediction/           Forecasts failures using historical patterns.
|   |                         Proactive actions before incidents occur.
|   +-- dev/                  Autonomous development agents:
|       |-- architect_agent.nc    Architecture analysis and component design.
|       |-- developer_agent.nc    Code/patch/config generation.
|       |-- reviewer_agent.nc     Automated code and config review.
|       |-- testing_agent.nc      Test generation and regression planning.
|       +-- deployment_agent.nc   Deployment planning and rollout monitoring.
|
|-- intelligence/             Higher-order reasoning.
|   |-- causal_reasoning/     Bayesian causal inference engine. Builds
|   |                         probabilistic models of cause-effect.
|   |-- observability/        Telemetry intelligence: anomaly detection,
|   |                         trend analysis, correlation, clustering.
|   +-- self_improvement/     RL-based self-improvement. Tunes swarm
|                             parameters based on historical performance.
|
|-- memory/                   Persistent knowledge stores.
|   |-- pheromone_graph/      Causal relationship graph. Edges weighted by
|   |                         success frequency. Stored as JSON files in
|   |                         memory/pheromone/edges/.
|   |-- knowledge_graph/      Entity-relationship store. Services, teams,
|   |                         patterns as nodes with typed relations.
|   |-- vector_store/         Semantic search (RAG). Embeddings for
|   |                         natural language incident queries.
|   +-- incident_db/          Incident history. Full records stored as
|                             JSON in incidents/ directory.
|
|-- digital_twin/             Live system topology model.
|   +-- system_model.nc       Service registry, dependency graph, health
|                             tracking, blast radius calculation.
|
|-- models/                   AI model interaction layer.
|   |-- reasoning_model/      Prompts for investigation hypotheses.
|   |-- prediction_model/     Prompts for failure forecasting.
|   +-- code_model/           Prompts for code/config generation.
|
|-- environment/              External system adapters.
|   |-- log_adapter/          Elasticsearch, Kubernetes logs.
|   |-- metrics_adapter/      Prometheus, custom health checks.
|   |-- trace_adapter/        Jaeger, OpenTelemetry.
|   +-- deployment_engine/    GitHub API, Kubernetes deployments.
|
|-- security/                 Governance layer.
|   |-- policy_engine/        RBAC policies, approval gates.
|   |-- sandbox/              Isolated fix testing environment.
|   +-- audit/                Immutable audit trail (who/what/when/where).
|
|-- simulation/               Testing environment.
|   |-- simulator.nc          Generates synthetic incidents.
|   +-- scenarios/            Pre-built failure scenarios.
|
|-- sdk/                      Extension points.
|   |-- agent_template.nc     Boilerplate for new agent types.
|   +-- plugin_api.nc         Plugin registration and lifecycle.
|
|-- tests/                    All test suites.
|-- docs/                     Documentation.
|-- k8s/                      Kubernetes manifests.
|-- Dockerfile                Multi-stage production build.
+-- docker-compose.yml        Full stack definition.
```

---

## How Agents Work

### Agent Lifecycle

1. **Spawn**: `POST /agents/spawn` with `type` and optional `id`. The kernel creates an agent state file in `agents_state/` and registers the agent in the runtime.

2. **Run**: The agent receives tasks through the scheduler. Each agent type has specialized functions that call AI models, query external systems, and write results.

3. **Communicate**: Agents publish messages to the message bus (`agents_state/bus/`). Other agents subscribe to topics and react.

4. **Kill**: `POST /agents/kill` with `id`. The kernel marks the agent as terminated and removes it from the active registry.

### Agent State

Each running agent has a state file at `agents_state/{agent_id}.json`:

```json
{
  "id": "det-001",
  "type": "detection",
  "status": "running",
  "spawned_at": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z",
  "task_count": 5,
  "last_active": "2024-01-15T10:35:00Z"
}
```

### Agent Communication

Agents communicate via the message bus:

```
Agent A --[publish "anomaly-detected"]--> Bus --> Agent B (subscribed)
```

Messages are persisted in `agents_state/bus/{topic}.json` as arrays. This enables asynchronous, decoupled communication between agent types.

### Investigation Pipeline Flow

```
Detection --> Investigation --> Root Cause (ACO) --> Fix Generation (ABC)
    |                                                       |
    |                                                       v
    |                                                 Validation (Sandbox)
    |                                                       |
    |                                                       v
    +-- Learning <-- Feedback <--------------------- Execution/Report
```

Each step in the pipeline can operate independently or be chained together via the `/investigate` or `/self-heal` endpoints which orchestrate the full flow.

---

## Swarm Algorithms

### Ant Colony Optimization (ACO)

**Purpose**: Discover root cause paths through the system dependency graph.

**How it works**:

1. **Initialize**: Create N ant agents (default 50, configured by `ANT_COLONY_SIZE`).

2. **Explore**: Each ant traverses the pheromone graph from the symptom node. At each node, the ant chooses the next node probabilistically:

   ```
   P(next) = (pheromone[edge]^alpha) * (heuristic[edge]^beta) / sum
   ```

   - `alpha` (default 1.0): Weight given to pheromone (past experience)
   - `beta` (default 2.0): Weight given to heuristic (current evidence)

3. **Evaluate**: Each ant's path is scored based on the AI's causal analysis of the traversed nodes.

4. **Reinforce**: Successful paths receive pheromone deposit proportional to their score. This makes future ants more likely to follow productive paths.

5. **Evaporate**: All pheromone decays by `(1 - PHEROMONE_DECAY_RATE)` each cycle. This prevents stale paths from dominating.

6. **Converge**: After `ANT_MAX_ITERATIONS` cycles, the highest-pheromone path from symptom to root cause is returned.

**Pheromone Graph**: Stored in `memory/pheromone/edges/` as JSON files. Each edge file contains:

```json
{
  "from": "error_spike",
  "to": "db_connection_failure",
  "score": 4.5,
  "last_updated": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z"
}
```

### Artificial Bee Colony (ABC)

**Purpose**: Optimize remediation strategies.

**How it works**:

1. **Scout Phase** (`BEE_SCOUT_COUNT` bees): Scouts explore the solution space by generating diverse fix strategies using AI. Each scout proposes a different approach (rollback, config change, scale up, restart, etc.).

2. **Worker Phase** (`BEE_WORKER_COUNT` bees): Workers evaluate each scout's solution for:
   - Safety (will it cause downtime?)
   - Effectiveness (will it fix the root cause?)
   - Reversibility (can it be undone?)
   - Speed (time to resolution)

3. **Evaluator Phase** (`BEE_EVALUATOR_COUNT` bees): Evaluators rank all solutions and select the optimal fix. If a solution has been evaluated `BEE_ABANDONMENT_LIMIT` times without improvement, it is abandoned and a new scout explores a replacement.

4. **Output**: The best fix with full execution plan, alternative fixes, and risk assessment.

### Why ACO + ABC Together

```
ACO finds WHAT is wrong  -->  ABC finds HOW to fix it
    (explore quickly)            (optimize safely)
```

ACO excels at exploration (finding root causes in complex graphs). ABC excels at exploitation (optimizing solutions within a solution space). Together, they provide both fast diagnosis and safe remediation.

---

## Cognitive Memory System

HiveANT uses a 5-layer cognitive memory model inspired by human memory:

### 1. Working Memory

**What**: Current investigation signals and context.
**Where**: In-memory during active investigation.
**Lifetime**: Duration of a single investigation.

When an investigation starts, all collected signals (logs, metrics, traces) are held in working memory. This is passed between agent stages.

### 2. Episodic Memory

**What**: Full records of past incidents.
**Where**: `incidents/` directory as JSON files.
**Lifetime**: Persistent (subject to retention policy).

Each resolved incident is stored with the full timeline: detection, investigation, root cause, fix applied, outcome. This allows learning from specific past events.

### 3. Semantic Memory

**What**: Generalized patterns extracted from incidents.
**Where**: `knowledge/` directory.
**Lifetime**: Persistent, grows over time.

AI extracts patterns like "database credential changes cause 5xx errors" from multiple incidents. These generalizations help future investigations skip known paths.

### 4. Procedural Memory

**What**: Learned fix runbooks and action sequences.
**Where**: `knowledge/` directory (procedures).
**Lifetime**: Persistent, versioned.

When a fix works, the exact steps are stored as a procedure. Next time a similar issue is detected, the system can apply the known fix without full AI reasoning.

### 5. RL Q-Table

**What**: State-action values for swarm parameter tuning.
**Where**: `agents_state/` (Q-table file).
**Formula**: `Q(s,a) = Q(s,a) + alpha * (reward - Q(s,a))`

The reinforcement learning layer tracks which swarm configurations work best for different incident types. Over time, the system automatically tunes ACO/ABC parameters for optimal performance.

**Parameters**:
- `RL_ALPHA` (0.1): Learning rate. Higher = faster adaptation, less stability.
- `RL_EPSILON` (0.2): Exploration rate. 20% of the time, try a random configuration to discover improvements.

---

## Digital Twin

The digital twin (`digital_twin/system_model.nc`) maintains a live model of your infrastructure.

### Service Registration

Register services with their type and metadata:

```bash
curl -X POST http://localhost:7700/twin/register \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"id": "checkout-api", "type": "api", "dependencies": [], "metadata": {"team": "platform"}}'
```

### Dependency Tracking

Add dependencies between services:

```bash
curl -X POST http://localhost:7700/twin/dependency \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"from": "checkout-api", "to": "postgres-db", "type": "database"}'
```

### Blast Radius Analysis

When a service fails, the digital twin calculates the impact:

```bash
curl -X POST http://localhost:7700/twin/impact \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"service": "postgres-db"}'
```

Returns all upstream services affected, ordered by distance.

### Topology View

```bash
curl http://localhost:7700/twin/topology
```

Returns the full service graph with health status.

**Storage**: Service models stored in `memory/twins/services/` as JSON files.

---

## Adding a New Agent

### Step 1: Create the Agent File

Create `agents/my_type/my_agent.nc`:

```nc
// agents/my_type/my_agent.nc
// My Custom Agent -- does something useful

to my_agent_analyze with target, context, options:
    purpose: "Analyze target system for custom patterns"

    // Build AI prompt
    set system_prompt to "You are a specialized analysis agent. Return JSON."
    set user_prompt to "Analyze " + target + " for the following:\n"
    user_prompt = user_prompt + "Context: " + str(context) + "\n"
    user_prompt = user_prompt + "Return JSON with: analysis, findings, recommendations"

    // Call AI model
    set ai_result to ai(system_prompt, user_prompt)
    set parsed to json_decode(ai_result)

    // Enrich with metadata
    set result to {
        "agent": "my_type",
        "target": target,
        "analysis": parsed.analysis,
        "findings": parsed.findings,
        "recommendations": parsed.recommendations,
        "analyzed_at": time_iso()
    }

    respond with result


to my_agent_report with target:
    purpose: "Generate a report for target"

    // Load relevant memory
    set memory to load_cognitive_memory(target)

    set prompt to "Generate a report for " + target
    set ai_result to ai("You generate reports. Return JSON.", prompt)

    respond with json_decode(ai_result)
```

### Step 2: Add Routes in server.nc

Add route handlers that call your agent functions:

```nc
route POST "/my-agent/analyze":
    set result to my_agent_analyze(body.target, body.context, body.options)
    respond with result

route GET "/my-agent/report":
    set result to my_agent_report(query.target)
    respond with result
```

### Step 3: Add to Agent Registry

In the `spawn_agent` function in `server.nc`, add your type to the switch:

```nc
if type is equal "my_type":
    // Initialize agent-specific state
    set agent.capabilities to ["analyze", "report"]
```

### Step 4: Write Tests

Add to `tests/test_agents.nc`:

```nc
describe "My Agent -- Analysis":
    it "should analyze a target":
        set result to my_agent_analyze("test-service", "test context", "")
        assert result.agent is equal "my_type"
        assert result.findings is not equal ""
    it "should handle empty context":
        set result to my_agent_analyze("test-service", "", "")
        assert result is not equal ""

describe "My Agent -- Report":
    it "should generate report":
        set result to my_agent_report("test-service")
        assert result is not equal ""
```

### Step 5: Document

Add the agent to `docs/API_REFERENCE.md` and update the README agent table.

---

## Adding a New Integration

Integrations are external system adapters in the `environment/` directory.

### Step 1: Create the Adapter

Create `environment/my_adapter/my_adapter.nc`:

```nc
// environment/my_adapter/my_adapter.nc
// Adapter for MySystem

to my_adapter_query with query_params:
    purpose: "Query MySystem for data"

    set url to env("MY_SYSTEM_URL")
    set token to env("MY_SYSTEM_TOKEN")

    if url is equal "":
        respond with {"error": "MY_SYSTEM_URL not configured", "data": []}

    set headers to {"Authorization": "Bearer " + token}
    set response to http_get(url + "/api/query", headers)

    respond with json_decode(response)


to my_adapter_push with data:
    purpose: "Push data to MySystem"

    set url to env("MY_SYSTEM_URL")
    set token to env("MY_SYSTEM_TOKEN")

    set headers to {"Authorization": "Bearer " + token, "Content-Type": "application/json"}
    set response to http_post(url + "/api/data", json_encode(data), headers)

    respond with json_decode(response)
```

### Step 2: Add Environment Variables

Add to `config/.env.example`:

```
# -- MySystem Integration --
MY_SYSTEM_URL=
MY_SYSTEM_TOKEN=
```

### Step 3: Wire into Investigation Pipeline

If the adapter should be used during investigations, import it in the relevant agent (e.g., `investigation_agent.nc`) and call it during signal collection.

### Step 4: Add Routes (optional)

If the adapter should be directly accessible via API:

```nc
route POST "/my-system/query":
    set result to my_adapter_query(body.params)
    respond with result
```

## API Reference

### Request/Response Examples

#### Initialize Kernel

```bash
curl -X POST http://localhost:7700/kernel/init
```

Response:
```json
{
  "kernel": {
    "name": "HiveANT",
    "version": "1.0.0",
    "status": "running"
  },
  "scheduler": "initialized",
  "pheromone_db": "initialized",
  "digital_twin": "initialized",
  "stability": "initialized",
  "file_write_verified": true
}
```

#### Spawn Agent

```bash
curl -X POST http://localhost:7700/agents/spawn \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"type": "detection", "id": "det-001"}'
```

Response:
```json
{
  "id": "det-001",
  "type": "detection",
  "status": "running",
  "spawned_at": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z"
}
```

#### Full Investigation

```bash
curl -X POST http://localhost:7700/investigate \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"service": "checkout-api", "description": "HTTP 500 errors after deploy v2.4.1"}'
```

Response:
```json
{
  "incident_id": "INC-20240115-001",
  "service": "checkout-api",
  "summary": "Root cause identified with 92% confidence",
  "root_cause": "Database credential mismatch after deploy v2.4.1",
  "category": "configuration",
  "confidence_percent": 92,
  "recommended_fix": {
    "description": "Rollback database credentials to pre-deploy values",
    "commands": [
      {"cmd": "kubectl rollout undo deploy/checkout-api", "risk": "low"}
    ]
  },
  "alternative_fixes": [...],
  "pheromone_updates": [...],
  "timeline": [...]
}
```

#### Add Pheromone Edge

```bash
curl -X POST http://localhost:7700/pheromone/add \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"from": "error_spike", "to": "db_credential_change", "score": 2.5}'
```

Response:
```json
{
  "from": "error_spike",
  "to": "db_credential_change",
  "score": 2.5,
  "status": "added"
}
```

#### Predict Failures

```bash
curl -X POST http://localhost:7700/predict \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"service": "checkout-api", "horizon": "24h"}'
```

Response:
```json
{
  "service": "checkout-api",
  "horizon": "24h",
  "risk_score": 35,
  "risk_level": "medium",
  "predictions": [
    {
      "type": "memory_pressure",
      "probability": 0.45,
      "estimated_time": "6-12 hours"
    }
  ],
  "proactive_actions": [
    "Scale pods to 4 replicas",
    "Enable memory limit alerts at 80%"
  ]
}
```

#### Sandbox Test

```bash
curl -X POST http://localhost:7700/sandbox/test \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{
    "commands": [{"cmd": "kubectl rollout undo deploy/checkout", "description": "Rollback"}],
    "service": "checkout-api"
  }'
```

Response:
```json
{
  "overall_safe": true,
  "results": [
    {
      "command": "kubectl rollout undo deploy/checkout",
      "safe": true,
      "risk": "low",
      "analysis": "Rollback to previous revision is safe"
    }
  ],
  "recommendation": "Safe to execute"
}
```

#### Authentication

```bash
# Register first user (bootstrap)
curl -X POST http://localhost:7700/auth/register \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"username": "admin", "password": "secure-password", "role": "admin", "org_id": "my-org"}'

# Login
curl -X POST http://localhost:7700/auth/login \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -d '{"username": "admin", "password": "secure-password"}'

# Use token for authenticated endpoints
curl -X POST http://localhost:7700/agents/spawn \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -H "Authorization: Bearer <token>" \
  -d '{"type": "detection", "id": "det-001"}'
```

---

## Testing Guide

### Test File Structure

NC test files use `describe` / `it` / `assert` syntax:

```nc
describe "Feature Name":
    it "should do something":
        set result to some_function("input")
        assert result.field is equal "expected"
    it "should handle edge case":
        set result to some_function("")
        assert result.error is not equal ""
```

### Running Tests

```bash
# All tests via start.sh
./start.sh test

# Individual NC test file
NC_ALLOW_EXEC=1 NC_ALLOW_FILE_WRITE=1 nc test tests/test_hiveant.nc

# Shell-based API tests (requires running server)
bash tests/test_api.sh
```

### Test Suites

| File | Purpose | Requires Server |
|------|---------|----------------|
| `test_hiveant.nc` | Core system: kernel, auth, pheromone, twin, RBAC | No |
| `test_agents.nc` | All 12 agent types and cross-agent integration | No |
| `test_core.nc` | Kernel internals, registry, memory, digital twin | No |
| `test_api.sh` | HTTP endpoint integration | Yes |
| `test_e2e_pipeline.sh` | Full detection-to-resolution pipeline | Yes |
| `test_performance.sh` | Throughput, latency, concurrent agents | Yes |
| `test_security.sh` | Injection, traversal, SSRF, auth bypass | Yes |

### Writing New Tests

1. **Unit tests**: Add to the appropriate `.nc` test file. Test one function at a time.
2. **Integration tests**: Add to `test_agents.nc` under the "Integration" section for cross-agent flows.
3. **API tests**: Add curl commands to `test_api.sh`.
4. **Always test**: Valid input, empty/missing input, error conditions, edge cases.

### Assert Syntax

```nc
assert result is equal "value"           // Exact match
assert result is not equal ""            // Not empty
assert result.count is above 0           // Greater than
assert result.count is above -1          // Greater than or equal to 0
```

---

## Coding Conventions

- **NC files**: Use `snake_case` for function and variable names.
- **Purpose comments**: Every function should have a `purpose:` line.
- **Error handling**: Use `try/otherwise` for file operations and external calls.
- **Input sanitization**: Always sanitize user-supplied IDs with `safe_id()` or `sanitize()`.
- **Audit logging**: Log all state-changing operations via the audit module.
- **File-based locking**: Use lock files for read-modify-write operations on shared state.

---

*For more information, see the [README](../README.md), [API Reference](API_REFERENCE.md), and [User Manual](USER_MANUAL.md).*

# HiveANT — Go-To-Market Strategy & Product Overview

## One-Line Pitch

> **HiveANT resolves production incidents before your engineers wake up.**

Not monitoring. Not alerting. Not dashboards. **Autonomous resolution.**

---

## Product Vision

HiveANT is the first **Swarm Autonomous AI Operating System** for software infrastructure. It coordinates thousands of AI agents using biological swarm algorithms (Ant Colony Optimization + Bee Colony Optimization) to autonomously investigate, diagnose, fix, and learn from production failures.

The core innovation: **a biological memory model that compounds with every incident.** Incident #1 takes 60 seconds. Incident #50 of the same class takes 5 seconds. No retraining. No configuration. The system learns like a living organism.

---

## System Architecture

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                                                                         │
│                     HIVEANT SWARM OPERATING SYSTEM                      │
│                                                                         │
│  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐    │
│  │                    SWARM OS KERNEL                               │    │

│  │  │  Agent     │  │  Task     │  │  Swarm    │  │  Message   │  │    │
│  │  │  Runtime   │  │ Scheduler │  │ Stability │  │  Bus       │  │    │
```

---

## Incident Resolution Flow

```
          ┌──────────────┐
          │  ALERT FIRES  │  (PagerDuty, Prometheus, Slack, webhook)
          └──────┬───────┘
                 │
                 ▼
     ┌───────────────────────┐
     │  1. DETECT             │  Detection agents monitor health
     │     Anomaly spotted    │  endpoints, error rates, latency
     │     Severity assessed  │  
     └───────────┬───────────┘
                 │
                 ▼
     ┌───────────────────────┐
     │  2. INVESTIGATE        │  Investigation agents pull:
     │     Pull telemetry     │  • Prometheus metrics
     │     from all sources   │  • Elasticsearch logs
     │                        │  • GitHub deploy history
     │                        │  • Health check responses
     └───────────┬───────────┘
                 │
                 ▼
     ┌───────────────────────┐
     │  3. ROOT CAUSE (ACO)   │  50 ant agents explore causal
     │                        │  paths through the system graph
     │  error_spike           │
     │     ↓ (0.3)           │  Each ant builds:
     │  conn_pool_exhausted   │    symptom → intermediate → root
     │     ↓ (0.7)           │
     │  credential_mismatch   │  Best path = highest pheromone
     │     ↓ (0.9)           │  Confidence: 87%
     │  deploy_v2.4.1  ←ROOT │
     └───────────┬───────────┘
                 │
                 ▼
     ┌───────────────────────┐
     │  4. FIX (ABC)          │  Bee colony optimization:
     │                        │
     │  Scout: 5 strategies   │  1. Rollback deploy (safe, fast)
     │  Worker: Score each    │  2. Fix credentials (risky)
     │  Evaluator: Best fix   │  3. Scale + retry (slow)
     │                        │  4. Config patch (medium)
     │  Winner: Rollback      │  5. Restart pods (blunt)
     │  Confidence: 92%       │
     │  Risk: LOW             │
     └───────────┬───────────┘
                 │
                 ▼
     ┌───────────────────────┐
     │  5. VALIDATE           │  Sandbox tests the fix:
     │     Dry-run in sandbox │  • Predicts outcome
     │     Check side effects │  • Checks for regressions
     │     Verify rollback    │  • Validates rollback works
     └───────────┬───────────┘
                 │
                 ▼
     ┌───────────────────────┐
     │  6. APPLY              │  Execute fix commands:
     │     kubectl rollout    │  • Pre-checks pass
     │     undo deploy/       │  • Commands run
     │     checkout-api       │  • Post-checks verify
     │                        │  • Rollback ready if needed
     └───────────┬───────────┘
                 │
                 ▼
     ┌───────────────────────┐
     │  7. VERIFY             │  Confirm recovery:
     │     Error rate → 0%    │  • Metrics back to normal
     │     Latency → normal   │  • No new errors
     │     Health → 200       │  • Service responding
     └───────────┬───────────┘
                 │
                 ▼
     ┌───────────────────────┐
     │  8. LEARN              │  Update all memory:
     │     ✓ Pheromone path   │  • Reinforce causal path
     │       reinforced       │  • Save pattern to semantic
     │     ✓ Pattern saved    │  • Save runbook to procedural
     │     ✓ Runbook saved    │  • Update RL Q-table
     │     ✓ RL updated       │
     │                        │  NEXT TIME: 5 seconds
     │     This time: 60s     │  instead of 60
     └───────────────────────┘
```

---

## Pheromone Memory — How It Learns

```
                    INCIDENT #1                          INCIDENT #50
                    (First encounter)                    (Same class)

                    Confidence: 45%                      Confidence: 94%
                    Time: 60 seconds                     Time: 5 seconds

    error_spike ──────────→ error_spike
        │ score: 0.3                │ score: 4.7  ████████████
        ▼                           ▼
    conn_pool ────────────→ conn_pool
        │ score: 0.5                │ score: 6.2  ████████████████
        ▼                           ▼
    credential_mismatch ──→ credential_mismatch
        │ score: 0.7                │ score: 8.1  ██████████████████████
        ▼                           ▼
    deploy_change ────────→ deploy_change
        │ score: 0.2                │ score: 9.3  █████████████████████████
        ▼                           ▼
    ROOT CAUSE             ROOT CAUSE (instant)

    ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │  Each successful resolution REINFORCES the path.     │
    │  Each failure lets the path DECAY.                   │
    │  After 50 incidents, the swarm KNOWS the answer.     │
    │                                                      │
    │  No retraining. No configuration. No human input.    │
    │  The system evolves like a biological organism.       │
    └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

## Competitive Landscape

```
                        Autonomous Resolution
                              ▲
                              │
                     HiveANT  │  ★
                   (ACO+ABC+  │
                    Learning) │
                              │
                              │         Dynatrace Davis
                              │         (ML-based)
                              │
          Moogsoft ───────────┼─────────────────────── Intelligence
          (Correlation)       │
                              │
                              │
     PagerDuty ───────────────┼──── BigPanda
     (Alert routing)          │     (Event correlation)
                              │
                              │
     Grafana ─────────────────┼──── Datadog
     (Dashboards)             │     (Monitoring)
                              │
                              ▼
                        Manual Dashboards
```

### What Each Competitor Does vs HiveANT

| Tool | What They Do | Where They Stop | HiveANT Goes Further |
|------|-------------|----------------|---------------------|
| **PagerDuty** | Routes alerts to humans | Alert delivered | Resolves incident autonomously |
| **Datadog** | Shows dashboards + anomalies | "Here's a graph" | "Here's the root cause and the fix" |
| **Dynatrace** | ML-based root cause suggestions | "Probable cause: X" | "Root cause: X, fix: Y, applied, verified" |
| **Moogsoft** | Correlates events, reduces noise | "These 50 alerts are related" | "They're related because of this causal chain, and here's the fix" |
| **Splunk ITSI** | Log analysis + correlation | "Interesting pattern found" | "Pattern matches semantic memory, confidence 94%, auto-resolving" |

### The Moat: What No Competitor Can Copy Quickly

1. **Pheromone Memory** — Self-improving causal graph that compounds. Can't be replicated with traditional ML.
2. **Dual Swarm (ACO + ABC)** — Two biological algorithms working in tandem. ACO for discovery, ABC for optimization. Published computer science applied to operations.
3. **Full Autonomy Pipeline** — Detect → Investigate → Root Cause → Fix → Validate → Apply → Learn. Nobody else does all 7 steps.
4. **Zero-Config Learning** — No training data, no model fine-tuning, no ML pipeline. Just run it and it learns from your incidents.
